help 2020-12-09 18:20:46 conveyor engines have only 2 downsides, it making the plane pitch slightly up or down depending on the center of lift, and it making you lose roll control (happens when the conveyor/piston glitches into the block on front of it.) however, it does make you fly smoothly without lag, which can help if you dont have a strong computer. If you arent into that, then conveyor engines speed can be easily set and dont take up as much space as super rocket engine spam.

Base your carrier off of 3d models and paint accordingly. Make sure everything is proportionate. For elevators, use ropes and suspension to pull the elevators up and down. help 2021-03-12 18:24:58 (The motor is the circle) 
1: The motor is located at the back of the beam. This is the least stable, and the motor has to work extra hard to lift and move the beam.
2: This is the most ideal. While the front is still heavy, the motor being placed somewhere between the center and back of the beam means that the back can cancel out weight at the front. 
3: This is the most stable design, but it doesnt really work with your missile truck thing. I suggest number 2

creations-chat 2022-10-11 23:27:07 Do Tutorials encourage the lazy to hop into any server and make something that they didn‚Äôt come up themselves. It can be somewhat useful for the newer players but what are the odds of someone new actually learning something if they don‚Äôt understand the concepts behind the techniques and mechanics? Tutorials can be comparable to water, it can help you when you need it, but can kill your if used incorrectly or against you. In this situation, a tutorial can be useful for some, but would just be a free plane for everyone to use and lose the specialty behind the build and/or would be ruined by those who use it. In the long run, a tutorial would just make the PC community worse since the more tutorials there are, the more people who become lazy, not willing to learn/do things like building what they want themselves, and dependent on those who make tutorials to create more. You can already see this happening with TheMadVulpen and the majority of his fanbase.?
